***поминать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a> (10274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pominátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помянуть.html>помяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember, to recall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mention
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихо.html>ли́хом</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>pomináj</b> menjá líxom!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">remember me kindly! (<i>sometimes used when someone leaves for a very risky venture or leaves for good</i>)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pray for the health living or the repose of the soul of the dead, to commemorate</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pominátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помять.html>помя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to squeeze, to press, to wrinkle for awhile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:перчатка.html>перча́тки</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвечать.html>отвеча́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On stojál dólgo, <b>pominája</b> perčátki, ne znál, što otvečátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He stood for a long time, wrinkling his gloves, and did not know how to reply.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***поминки.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поминки.html>поми́нки</a> (11768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминать.html>помина́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pominátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминки.html>поми́нки</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomínki</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поминки.html>поми́нок</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-wake">wake, funeral repast</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">помири́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>помни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мнить.html>мнить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or high-style</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think, to consider, to imagine</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>по́мнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pómnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помниться.html>по́мниться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pómnitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запомниться.html>запо́мниться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember, to recollect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:помниться.html>по́мнится</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тогда.html>тогда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понравиться.html>понра́вилась</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Pómnitsja</b>, oná tebé togdá ponrávilasʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I remember that you liked her then.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>по́мнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pómnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p>

***помогать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помогать.html>помога́ть</a> (882)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">pomagati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помогать.html>помога́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomogátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>помо́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to help (+ dative)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помогать.html>помога́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja jemú <b>pomogál</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was helping him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to aid, to assist (+ dative)</li>
<li>to avail (+ dative)</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмога.html>подмо́га</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podmóga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощник.html>помо́щник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomóšnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помойный.html>помо́йный</a> (17037)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помои.html>помо́и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomói</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***помолодеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помолодеть.html>помолоде́ть</a> (16509)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодеть.html>молоде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">molodétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помолодеть.html>помолоде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomolodétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодеть.html>молоде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become younger
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:казаться.html>ка́жется</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помолодеть.html>помолоде́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne kážetsja, što ja <b>pomolodél</b> na désjatʹ let</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I feel like I am ten years younger</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***помочь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>по́мочь</a> (1225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мочь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">močʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*megʰ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">might</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>помо́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomóčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помогать.html>помога́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to help (+ dative)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>помо́чь</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú tebé <b>pomóčʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I want <b>to help</b> you.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to aid, to assist (+ dative)</li>
<li>to avail (+ dative)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощник.html>помо́щник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomóščnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощница.html>помо́щница</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomóščnica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pómoščʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pomoťь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pómoščʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>по́мочь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pómočʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>по́мочи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>по́мочи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>по́мочей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> belt, tape, or restraint to hold, support, or suspend something or someone <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also figurative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> suspenders (US), braces (Britain)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually plural</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> leading-string</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete  or  regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a gathering of friends and neighbors to help in some project <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">such as a quilting bee, a barn-raising bee</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete  or  regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> synonymous with <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pómoščʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>: help, assistance, aid, support</li></ol>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li>посодействовать, поспособствовать, пособить, <a href = vnd.unilang:подсобить.html>подсоби́ть</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pómoščʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Pronunciation from native <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">помо́чник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomóčnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощник.html>помо́щник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomóščnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощник.html>помо́щника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощник.html>помо́щники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощник.html>помо́щников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощница.html>помо́щница</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>associate, assistant, deputy</li>
<li>helper, aid</li>
<li>helpmate</li></ol>

***помощь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a> (409)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomoštĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pomoťь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помочь.html>по́мочь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pómočʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pómoščʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>help, assistance, aid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спасибо.html>спаси́бо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Spasíbo za <b>pómoščʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Thanks for <b>the help</b>!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нуждаться.html>нужда́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посторонний.html>посторо́нней</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощи</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On nuždájetsja v postorónnej <b>pómošči</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He needs (external) help.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>relief</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помрачение.html>помраче́ние</a> (20601)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">помрачи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pomračítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помрачение.html>помраче́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomračénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помрачение.html>помраче́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помрачение.html>помраче́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помрачение.html>помраче́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>darkening</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> exceeding, overshadowing</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> obscuring</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> saddening</li>
<li>darkness, gloom</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:помрачнеть.html>помрачне́ть</a> (11989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мрачнеть.html>мрачне́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mračnétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помрачнеть.html>помрачне́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pomračnétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мрачнеть.html>мрачне́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become gloomy, to darken</li></ol>
